\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00063}00063 \# If the CREATE\_SUBDIRS tag is set to YES then doxygen will create 4096 sub-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00064}00064 \# directories (in 2 levels) under the output directory of each output format and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00065}00065 \# will distribute the generated files over these directories. Enabling this}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00066}00066 \# option can be useful when feeding doxygen a huge amount of source files, where}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00067}00067 \# putting all generated files in the same directory would otherwise causes}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00068}00068 \# performance problems for the file system.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00081}00081 \# The OUTPUT\_LANGUAGE tag is used to specify the language in which all}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00082}00082 \# documentation generated by doxygen is written. Doxygen will use this}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00083}00083 \# information to generate all constant output in the proper language.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00084}00084 \# Possible values are: Afrikaans, Arabic, Armenian, Brazilian, Catalan, Chinese,}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00091}00091 \# Ukrainian and Vietnamese.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00092}00092 \# The default value is: English.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00110}00110 REPEAT\_BRIEF           = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00111}00111 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00112}00112 \# This tag implements a quasi-\/intelligent brief description abbreviator that is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00113}00113 \# used to form the text in various listings. Each string in this list, if found}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00114}00114 \# as the leading text of the brief description, will be stripped from the text}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00115}00115 \# and the result, after processing the whole list, is used as the annotated}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00116}00116 \# text. Otherwise, the brief description is used as-\/is. If left blank, the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00117}00117 \# following values are used (\$name is automatically replaced with the name of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00118}00118 \# the entity):The \$name class, The \$name widget, The \$name file, is, provides,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00119}00119 \# specifies, contains, represents, a, an and the.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00120}00120 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00121}00121 ABBREVIATE\_BRIEF       = "{}The \$name class"{} \(\backslash\)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00123}00123                          "{}The \$name file"{} \(\backslash\)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00127}00127                          contains \(\backslash\)}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00155}00155 \# The STRIP\_FROM\_PATH tag can be used to strip a user-\/defined part of the path.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00156}00156 \# Stripping is only done if one of the specified strings matches the left-\/hand}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00157}00157 \# part of the path. The tag can be used to show relative paths in the file list.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00158}00158 \# If left blank the directory from which doxygen is run is used as the path to}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00162}00162 \# will be relative from the directory where doxygen is started.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00163}00163 \# This tag requires that the tag FULL\_PATH\_NAMES is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00164}00164 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00167}00167 \# The STRIP\_FROM\_INC\_PATH tag can be used to strip a user-\/defined part of the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00168}00168 \# path mentioned in the documentation of a class, which tells the reader which}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00169}00169 \# header file to include in order to use a class. If left blank only the name of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00170}00170 \# the header file containing the class definition is used. Otherwise one should}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00171}00171 \# specify the list of include paths that are normally passed to the compiler}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00172}00172 \# using the -\/I flag.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00173}00173 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00174}00174 STRIP\_FROM\_INC\_PATH    =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00175}00175 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00176}00176 \# If the SHORT\_NAMES tag is set to YES, doxygen will generate much shorter (but}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00177}00177 \# less readable) file names. This can be useful is your file systems doesn't}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00178}00178 \# support long names like on DOS, Mac, or CD-\/ROM.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00210}00210 \# The MULTILINE\_CPP\_IS\_BRIEF tag can be set to YES to make doxygen treat a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00211}00211 \# multi-\/line C++ special comment block (i.e. a block of //! or /// comments) as}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00243}00243 \# The TAB\_SIZE tag can be used to set the number of spaces in a tab. Doxygen}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00249}00249 \# This tag can be used to specify a number of aliases that act as commands in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00250}00250 \# the documentation. An alias has the form:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00251}00251 \# name=value}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00252}00252 \# For example adding}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00253}00253 \# "{}sideeffect=@par Side Effects:\string^\string^"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00254}00254 \# will allow you to put the command \(\backslash\)sideeffect (or @sideeffect) in the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00255}00255 \# documentation, which will result in a user-\/defined paragraph with heading}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00256}00256 \# "{}Side Effects:"{}. Note that you cannot put \(\backslash\)n's in the value part of an alias}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00257}00257 \# to insert newlines (in the resulting output). You can put \string^\string^ in the value part}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00258}00258 \# of an alias to insert a newline as if a physical newline was in the original}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00259}00259 \# file. When you need a literal \{ or \} or , in the value part of an alias you}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00260}00260 \# have to escape them by means of a backslash (\(\backslash\)), this can lead to conflicts}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00261}00261 \# with the commands \(\backslash\)\{ and \(\backslash\)\} for these it is advised to use the version @\{ and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00262}00262 \# @\} or use a double escape (\(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)\{ and \(\backslash\)\(\backslash\)\})}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00263}00263 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00264}00264 ALIASES                =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00265}00265 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00302}00302 \# Doxygen selects the parser to use depending on the extension of the files it}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00303}00303 \# parses. With this tag you can assign which parser to use for a given}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00304}00304 \# extension. Doxygen has a built-\/in mapping, but you can override or extend it}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00305}00305 \# using this tag. The format is ext=language, where ext is a file extension, and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00306}00306 \# language is one of the parsers supported by doxygen: IDL, Java, JavaScript,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00307}00307 \# Csharp (C\#), C, C++, Lex, D, PHP, md (Markdown), Objective-\/C, Python, Slice,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00308}00308 \# VHDL, Fortran (fixed format Fortran: FortranFixed, free formatted Fortran:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00309}00309 \# FortranFree, unknown formatted Fortran: Fortran. In the later case the parser}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00310}00310 \# tries to guess whether the code is fixed or free formatted code, this is the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00311}00311 \# default for Fortran type files). For instance to make doxygen treat .inc files}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00312}00312 \# as Fortran files (default is PHP), and .f files as C (default is Fortran),}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00313}00313 \# use: inc=Fortran f=C.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00314}00314 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00315}00315 \# Note: For files without extension you can use no\_extension as a placeholder.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00316}00316 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00317}00317 \# Note that for custom extensions you also need to set FILE\_PATTERNS otherwise}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00318}00318 \# the files are not read by doxygen. When specifying no\_extension you should add}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00319}00319 \# * to the FILE\_PATTERNS.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00320}00320 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00321}00321 \# Note see also the list of default file extension mappings.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00322}00322 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00344}00344 \# When enabled doxygen tries to link words that correspond to documented}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00345}00345 \# classes, or namespaces to their corresponding documentation. Such a link can}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00346}00346 \# be prevented in individual cases by putting a \% sign in front of the word or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00347}00347 \# globally by setting AUTOLINK\_SUPPORT to NO.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00351}00351 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00352}00352 \# If you use STL classes (i.e. std::string, std::vector, etc.) but do not want}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00353}00353 \# to include (a tag file for) the STL sources as input, then you should set this}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00354}00354 \# tag to YES in order to let doxygen match functions declarations and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00355}00355 \# definitions whose arguments contain STL classes (e.g. func(std::string);}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00356}00356 \# versus func(std::string) \{\}). This also make the inheritance and collaboration}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00357}00357 \# diagrams that involve STL classes more complete and accurate.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00358}00358 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00359}00359 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00364}00364 \# The default value is: NO.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00366}00366 CPP\_CLI\_SUPPORT        = NO}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00368}00368 \# Set the SIP\_SUPPORT tag to YES if your project consists of sip (see:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00369}00369 \# https://www.riverbankcomputing.com/software/sip/intro) sources only. Doxygen}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00370}00370 \# will parse them like normal C++ but will assume all classes use public instead}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00371}00371 \# of private inheritance when no explicit protection keyword is present.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00375}00375 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00376}00376 \# For Microsoft's IDL there are propget and propput attributes to indicate}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00377}00377 \# getter and setter methods for a property. Setting this option to YES will make}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00378}00378 \# doxygen to replace the get and set methods by a property in the documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00379}00379 \# This will only work if the methods are indeed getting or setting a simple}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00380}00380 \# type. If this is not the case, or you want to show the methods anyway, you}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00381}00381 \# should set this option to NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00382}00382 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00383}00383 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00384}00384 IDL\_PROPERTY\_SUPPORT   = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00385}00385 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00386}00386 \# If member grouping is used in the documentation and the DISTRIBUTE\_GROUP\_DOC}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00387}00387 \# tag is set to YES then doxygen will reuse the documentation of the first}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00388}00388 \# member in the group (if any) for the other members of the group. By default}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00389}00389 \# all members of a group must be documented explicitly.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00390}00390 \# The default value is: NO.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00393}00393 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00394}00394 \# If one adds a struct or class to a group and this option is enabled, then also}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00395}00395 \# any nested class or struct is added to the same group. By default this option}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00396}00396 \# is disabled and one has to add nested compounds explicitly via \(\backslash\)ingroup.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00397}00397 \# The default value is: NO.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00400}00400 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00401}00401 \# Set the SUBGROUPING tag to YES to allow class member groups of the same type}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00402}00402 \# (for instance a group of public functions) to be put as a subgroup of that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00403}00403 \# type (e.g. under the Public Functions section). Set it to NO to prevent}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00404}00404 \# subgrouping. Alternatively, this can be done per class using the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00405}00405 \# \(\backslash\)nosubgrouping command.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00406}00406 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00407}00407 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00408}00408 SUBGROUPING            = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00409}00409 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00410}00410 \# When the INLINE\_GROUPED\_CLASSES tag is set to YES, classes, structs and unions}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00411}00411 \# are shown inside the group in which they are included (e.g. using \(\backslash\)ingroup)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00412}00412 \# instead of on a separate page (for HTML and Man pages) or section (for LaTeX}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00413}00413 \# and RTF).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00414}00414 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00415}00415 \# Note that this feature does not work in combination with}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00416}00416 \# SEPARATE\_MEMBER\_PAGES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00417}00417 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00418}00418 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00419}00419 INLINE\_GROUPED\_CLASSES = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00420}00420 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00421}00421 \# When the INLINE\_SIMPLE\_STRUCTS tag is set to YES, structs, classes, and unions}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00422}00422 \# with only public data fields or simple typedef fields will be shown inline in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00423}00423 \# the documentation of the scope in which they are defined (i.e. file,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00424}00424 \# namespace, or group documentation), provided this scope is documented. If set}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00425}00425 \# to NO, structs, classes, and unions are shown on a separate page (for HTML and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00426}00426 \# Man pages) or section (for LaTeX and RTF).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00427}00427 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00428}00428 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00429}00429 INLINE\_SIMPLE\_STRUCTS  = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00430}00430 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00431}00431 \# When TYPEDEF\_HIDES\_STRUCT tag is enabled, a typedef of a struct, union, or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00432}00432 \# enum is documented as struct, union, or enum with the name of the typedef. So}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00433}00433 \# typedef struct TypeS \{\} TypeT, will appear in the documentation as a struct}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00434}00434 \# with name TypeT. When disabled the typedef will appear as a member of a file,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00435}00435 \# namespace, or class. And the struct will be named TypeS. This can typically be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00436}00436 \# useful for C code in case the coding convention dictates that all compound}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00437}00437 \# types are typedef'ed and only the typedef is referenced, never the tag name.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00438}00438 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00439}00439 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00440}00440 TYPEDEF\_HIDES\_STRUCT   = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00441}00441 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00442}00442 \# The size of the symbol lookup cache can be set using LOOKUP\_CACHE\_SIZE. This}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00443}00443 \# cache is used to resolve symbols given their name and scope. Since this can be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00444}00444 \# an expensive process and often the same symbol appears multiple times in the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00445}00445 \# code, doxygen keeps a cache of pre-\/resolved symbols. If the cache is too small}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00446}00446 \# doxygen will become slower. If the cache is too large, memory is wasted. The}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00447}00447 \# cache size is given by this formula: 2\string^(16+LOOKUP\_CACHE\_SIZE). The valid range}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00448}00448 \# is 0..9, the default is 0, corresponding to a cache size of 2\string^16=65536}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00449}00449 \# symbols. At the end of a run doxygen will report the cache usage and suggest}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00450}00450 \# the optimal cache size from a speed point of view.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00451}00451 \# Minimum value: 0, maximum value: 9, default value: 0.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00452}00452 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00453}00453 LOOKUP\_CACHE\_SIZE      = 0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00454}00454 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00455}00455 \# The NUM\_PROC\_THREADS specifies the number threads doxygen is allowed to use}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00456}00456 \# during processing. When set to 0 doxygen will based this on the number of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00457}00457 \# cores available in the system. You can set it explicitly to a value larger}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00458}00458 \# than 0 to get more control over the balance between CPU load and processing}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00459}00459 \# speed. At this moment only the input processing can be done using multiple}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00460}00460 \# threads. Since this is still an experimental feature the default is set to 1,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00461}00461 \# which effectively disables parallel processing. Please report any issues you}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00462}00462 \# encounter. Generating dot graphs in parallel is controlled by the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00463}00463 \# DOT\_NUM\_THREADS setting.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00464}00464 \# Minimum value: 0, maximum value: 32, default value: 1.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00465}00465 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00466}00466 NUM\_PROC\_THREADS       = 1}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00467}00467 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00468}00468 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00469}00469 \# Build related configuration options}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00470}00470 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00472}00472 \# If the EXTRACT\_ALL tag is set to YES, doxygen will assume all entities in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00473}00473 \# documentation are documented, even if no documentation was available. Private}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00474}00474 \# class members and static file members will be hidden unless the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00475}00475 \# EXTRACT\_PRIVATE respectively EXTRACT\_STATIC tags are set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00476}00476 \# Note: This will also disable the warnings about undocumented members that are}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00477}00477 \# normally produced when WARNINGS is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00478}00478 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00479}00479 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00480}00480 EXTRACT\_ALL            = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00481}00481 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00482}00482 \# If the EXTRACT\_PRIVATE tag is set to YES, all private members of a class will}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00483}00483 \# be included in the documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00484}00484 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00485}00485 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00488}00488 \# If the EXTRACT\_PRIV\_VIRTUAL tag is set to YES, documented private virtual}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00489}00489 \# methods of a class will be included in the documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00490}00490 \# The default value is: NO.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00494}00494 \# If the EXTRACT\_PACKAGE tag is set to YES, all members with package or internal}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00500}00500 \# If the EXTRACT\_STATIC tag is set to YES, all static members of a file will be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00501}00501 \# included in the documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00502}00502 \# The default value is: NO.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00505}00505 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00506}00506 \# If the EXTRACT\_LOCAL\_CLASSES tag is set to YES, classes (and structs) defined}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00507}00507 \# locally in source files will be included in the documentation. If set to NO,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00508}00508 \# only classes defined in header files are included. Does not have any effect}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00513}00513 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00514}00514 \# This flag is only useful for Objective-\/C code. If set to YES, local methods,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00515}00515 \# which are defined in the implementation section but not in the interface are}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00516}00516 \# included in the documentation. If set to NO, only methods in the interface are}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00517}00517 \# included.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00518}00518 \# The default value is: NO.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00521}00521 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00522}00522 \# If this flag is set to YES, the members of anonymous namespaces will be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00523}00523 \# extracted and appear in the documentation as a namespace called}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00524}00524 \# 'anonymous\_namespace\{file\}', where file will be replaced with the base name of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00525}00525 \# the file that contains the anonymous namespace. By default anonymous namespace}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00526}00526 \# are hidden.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00527}00527 \# The default value is: NO.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00529}00529 EXTRACT\_ANON\_NSPACES   = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00530}00530 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00531}00531 \# If this flag is set to YES, the name of an unnamed parameter in a declaration}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00532}00532 \# will be determined by the corresponding definition. By default unnamed}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00533}00533 \# parameters remain unnamed in the output.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00537}00537 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00538}00538 \# If the HIDE\_UNDOC\_MEMBERS tag is set to YES, doxygen will hide all}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00539}00539 \# undocumented members inside documented classes or files. If set to NO these}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00540}00540 \# members will be included in the various overviews, but no documentation}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00541}00541 \# section is generated. This option has no effect if EXTRACT\_ALL is enabled.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00542}00542 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00543}00543 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00544}00544 HIDE\_UNDOC\_MEMBERS     = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00545}00545 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00546}00546 \# If the HIDE\_UNDOC\_CLASSES tag is set to YES, doxygen will hide all}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00547}00547 \# undocumented classes that are normally visible in the class hierarchy. If set}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00548}00548 \# to NO, these classes will be included in the various overviews. This option}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00549}00549 \# has no effect if EXTRACT\_ALL is enabled.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00550}00550 \# The default value is: NO.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00574}00574 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00575}00575 \# With the correct setting of option CASE\_SENSE\_NAMES doxygen will better be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00576}00576 \# able to match the capabilities of the underlying filesystem. In case the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00577}00577 \# filesystem is case sensitive (i.e. it supports files in the same directory}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00578}00578 \# whose names only differ in casing), the option must be set to YES to properly}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00579}00579 \# deal with such files in case they appear in the input. For filesystems that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00580}00580 \# are not case sensitive the option should be be set to NO to properly deal with}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00581}00581 \# output files written for symbols that only differ in casing, such as for two}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00582}00582 \# classes, one named CLASS and the other named Class, and to also support}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00583}00583 \# references to files without having to specify the exact matching casing. On}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00584}00584 \# Windows (including Cygwin) and MacOS, users should typically set this option}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00585}00585 \# to NO, whereas on Linux or other Unix flavors it should typically be set to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00586}00586 \# YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00587}00587 \# The default value is: system dependent.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00588}00588 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00589}00589 CASE\_SENSE\_NAMES       = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00590}00590 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00680}00680 \# If the STRICT\_PROTO\_MATCHING option is enabled and doxygen fails to do proper}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00681}00681 \# type resolution of all parameters of a function it will reject a match between}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00682}00682 \# the prototype and the implementation of a member function even if there is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00683}00683 \# only one candidate or it is obvious which candidate to choose by doing a}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00721}00721 \# The MAX\_INITIALIZER\_LINES tag determines the maximum number of lines that the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00722}00722 \# initial value of a variable or macro / define can have for it to appear in the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00723}00723 \# documentation. If the initializer consists of more lines than specified here}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00724}00724 \# it will be hidden. Use a value of 0 to hide initializers completely. The}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00725}00725 \# appearance of the value of individual variables and macros / defines can be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00726}00726 \# controlled using \(\backslash\)showinitializer or \(\backslash\)hideinitializer command in the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00727}00727 \# documentation regardless of this setting.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00728}00728 \# Minimum value: 0, maximum value: 10000, default value: 30.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00729}00729 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00739}00739 \# Set the SHOW\_FILES tag to NO to disable the generation of the Files page. This}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00740}00740 \# will remove the Files entry from the Quick Index and from the Folder Tree View}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00741}00741 \# (if specified).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00742}00742 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00743}00743 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00744}00744 SHOW\_FILES             = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00745}00745 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00746}00746 \# Set the SHOW\_NAMESPACES tag to NO to disable the generation of the Namespaces}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00747}00747 \# page. This will remove the Namespaces entry from the Quick Index and from the}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00751}00751 SHOW\_NAMESPACES        = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00752}00752 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00753}00753 \# The FILE\_VERSION\_FILTER tag can be used to specify a program or script that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00754}00754 \# doxygen should invoke to get the current version for each file (typically from}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00755}00755 \# the version control system). Doxygen will invoke the program by executing (via}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00756}00756 \# popen()) the command command input-\/file, where command is the value of the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00757}00757 \# FILE\_VERSION\_FILTER tag, and input-\/file is the name of an input file provided}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00758}00758 \# by doxygen. Whatever the program writes to standard output is used as the file}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00759}00759 \# version. For an example see the documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00760}00760 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00761}00761 FILE\_VERSION\_FILTER    =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00762}00762 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00763}00763 \# The LAYOUT\_FILE tag can be used to specify a layout file which will be parsed}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00764}00764 \# by doxygen. The layout file controls the global structure of the generated}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00765}00765 \# output files in an output format independent way. To create the layout file}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00766}00766 \# that represents doxygen's defaults, run doxygen with the -\/l option. You can}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00767}00767 \# optionally specify a file name after the option, if omitted DoxygenLayout.xml}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00768}00768 \# will be used as the name of the layout file. See also section "{}Changing the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00769}00769 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# layout of pages"{} for information.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00770}00770 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00771}00771 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# Note that if you run doxygen from a directory containing a file called}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00772}00772 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# DoxygenLayout.xml, doxygen will parse it automatically even if the LAYOUT\_FILE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00773}00773 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# tag is left empty.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00774}00774 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00777}00777 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The CITE\_BIB\_FILES tag can be used to specify one or more bib files containing}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00778}00778 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# the reference definitions. This must be a list of .bib files. The .bib}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00782}00782 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# LATEX\_BIB\_STYLE. To use this feature you need bibtex and perl available in the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00783}00783 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# search path. See also \(\backslash\)cite for info how to create references.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00807}00807 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# If the WARN\_IF\_UNDOCUMENTED tag is set to YES then doxygen will generate}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00808}00808 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# warnings for undocumented members. If EXTRACT\_ALL is set to YES then this flag}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00809}00809 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# will automatically be disabled.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00814}00814 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# If the WARN\_IF\_DOC\_ERROR tag is set to YES, doxygen will generate warnings for}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00815}00815 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# potential errors in the documentation, such as documenting some parameters in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00816}00816 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# a documented function twice, or documenting parameters that don't exist or}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00817}00817 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# using markup commands wrongly.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00818}00818 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The default value is: YES.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00821}00821 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00822}00822 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# If WARN\_IF\_INCOMPLETE\_DOC is set to YES, doxygen will warn about incomplete}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00823}00823 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# function parameter documentation. If set to NO, doxygen will accept that some}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00824}00824 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# parameters have no documentation without warning.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00825}00825 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The default value is: YES.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00826}00826 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00827}00827 \textcolor{preprocessor}{WARN\_IF\_INCOMPLETE\_DOC = YES}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00828}00828 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00829}00829 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# This WARN\_NO\_PARAMDOC option can be enabled to get warnings for functions that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00830}00830 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# are documented, but have no documentation for their parameters or return}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00831}00831 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# value. If set to NO, doxygen will only warn about wrong parameter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00832}00832 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# documentation, but not about the absence of documentation. If EXTRACT\_ALL is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00833}00833 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# set to YES then this flag will automatically be disabled. See also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00834}00834 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# WARN\_IF\_INCOMPLETE\_DOC}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00835}00835 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The default value is: NO.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00836}00836 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00837}00837 \textcolor{preprocessor}{WARN\_NO\_PARAMDOC       = NO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00838}00838 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00839}00839 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# If the WARN\_AS\_ERROR tag is set to YES then doxygen will immediately stop when}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00840}00840 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# a warning is encountered. If the WARN\_AS\_ERROR tag is set to FAIL\_ON\_WARNINGS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00841}00841 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# then doxygen will continue running as if WARN\_AS\_ERROR tag is set to NO, but}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00842}00842 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# at the end of the doxygen process doxygen will return with a non-\/zero status.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00843}00843 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# Possible values are: NO, YES and FAIL\_ON\_WARNINGS.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00844}00844 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The default value is: NO.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00845}00845 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00846}00846 \textcolor{preprocessor}{WARN\_AS\_ERROR          = NO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00847}00847 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00848}00848 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The WARN\_FORMAT tag determines the format of the warning messages that doxygen}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00849}00849 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# can produce. The string should contain the \$file, \$line, and \$text tags, which}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00850}00850 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# will be replaced by the file and line number from which the warning originated}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00851}00851 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# and the warning text. Optionally the format may contain \$version, which will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00852}00852 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# be replaced by the version of the file (if it could be obtained via}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00853}00853 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# FILE\_VERSION\_FILTER)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00854}00854 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The default value is: \$file:\$line: \$text.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00855}00855 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00856}00856 \textcolor{preprocessor}{WARN\_FORMAT            = "{}}\$file:\$line: \$text"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00857}00857 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00858}00858 \# The WARN\_LOGFILE tag can be used to specify a file to which warning and error}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00859}00859 \# messages should be written. If left blank the output is written to standard}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00860}00860 \# error (stderr).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00861}00861 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00862}00862 WARN\_LOGFILE           =}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00865}00865 \# Configuration options related to the input files}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00866}00866 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00867}00867 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00868}00868 \# The INPUT tag is used to specify the files and/or directories that contain}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00869}00869 \# documented source files. You may enter file names like myfile.cpp or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00870}00870 \# directories like /usr/src/myproject. Separate the files or directories with}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00871}00871 \# spaces. See also FILE\_PATTERNS and EXTENSION\_MAPPING}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00872}00872 \# Note: If this tag is empty the current directory is searched.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00873}00873 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00874}00874 INPUT                  =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00875}00875 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00876}00876 \# This tag can be used to specify the character encoding of the source files}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00877}00877 \# that doxygen parses. Internally doxygen uses the UTF-\/8 encoding. Doxygen uses}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00878}00878 \# libiconv (or the iconv built into libc) for the transcoding. See the libiconv}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00879}00879 \# documentation (see:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00880}00880 \# https://www.gnu.org/software/libiconv/) for the list of possible encodings.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00881}00881 \# The default value is: UTF-\/8.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00882}00882 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00883}00883 INPUT\_ENCODING         = UTF-\/8}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00884}00884 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00885}00885 \# If the value of the INPUT tag contains directories, you can use the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00886}00886 \# FILE\_PATTERNS tag to specify one or more wildcard patterns (like *.cpp and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00887}00887 \# *.h) to filter out the source-\/files in the directories.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00888}00888 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00889}00889 \# Note that for custom extensions or not directly supported extensions you also}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00890}00890 \# need to set EXTENSION\_MAPPING for the extension otherwise the files are not}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00891}00891 \# read by doxygen.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00892}00892 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00893}00893 \# Note the list of default checked file patterns might differ from the list of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00894}00894 \# default file extension mappings.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00895}00895 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00896}00896 \# If left blank the following patterns are tested:*.c, *.cc, *.cxx, *.cpp,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00897}00897 \# *.c++, *.java, *.ii, *.ixx, *.ipp, *.i++, *.inl, *.idl, *.ddl, *.odl, *.h,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00898}00898 \# *.hh, *.hxx, *.hpp, *.h++, *.l, *.cs, *.d, *.php, *.php4, *.php5, *.phtml,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00899}00899 \# *.inc, *.m, *.markdown, *.md, *.mm, *.dox (to be provided as doxygen C}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00900}00900 \# comment), *.py, *.pyw, *.f90, *.f95, *.f03, *.f08, *.f18, *.f, *.for, *.vhd,}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00950}00950 \# The RECURSIVE tag can be used to specify whether or not subdirectories should}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00951}00951 \# be searched for input files as well.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00952}00952 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00953}00953 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00955}00955 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00956}00956 \# The EXCLUDE tag can be used to specify files and/or directories that should be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00957}00957 \# excluded from the INPUT source files. This way you can easily exclude a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00958}00958 \# subdirectory from a directory tree whose root is specified with the INPUT tag.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00959}00959 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00960}00960 \# Note that relative paths are relative to the directory from which doxygen is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00961}00961 \# run.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00962}00962 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00963}00963 EXCLUDE                =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00964}00964 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00965}00965 \# The EXCLUDE\_SYMLINKS tag can be used to select whether or not files or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00966}00966 \# directories that are symbolic links (a Unix file system feature) are excluded}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00967}00967 \# from the input.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00968}00968 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00969}00969 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00970}00970 EXCLUDE\_SYMLINKS       = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00971}00971 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00972}00972 \# If the value of the INPUT tag contains directories, you can use the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00973}00973 \# EXCLUDE\_PATTERNS tag to specify one or more wildcard patterns to exclude}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00974}00974 \# certain files from those directories.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00975}00975 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00976}00976 \# Note that the wildcards are matched against the file with absolute path, so to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00977}00977 \# exclude all test directories for example use the pattern */test/*}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00978}00978 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00979}00979 EXCLUDE\_PATTERNS       =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00980}00980 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00981}00981 \# The EXCLUDE\_SYMBOLS tag can be used to specify one or more symbol names}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00982}00982 \# (namespaces, classes, functions, etc.) that should be excluded from the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00983}00983 \# output. The symbol name can be a fully qualified name, a word, or if the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00984}00984 \# wildcard * is used, a substring. Examples: ANamespace, AClass,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00985}00985 \# AClass::ANamespace, ANamespace::*Test}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00986}00986 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00987}00987 \# Note that the wildcards are matched against the file with absolute path, so to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00988}00988 \# exclude all test directories use the pattern */test/*}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00989}00989 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00990}00990 EXCLUDE\_SYMBOLS        =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00991}00991 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00992}00992 \# The EXAMPLE\_PATH tag can be used to specify one or more files or directories}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00993}00993 \# that contain example code fragments that are included (see the \(\backslash\)include}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00994}00994 \# command).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00995}00995 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00996}00996 EXAMPLE\_PATH           =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00997}00997 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00998}00998 \# If the value of the EXAMPLE\_PATH tag contains directories, you can use the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l00999}00999 \# EXAMPLE\_PATTERNS tag to specify one or more wildcard pattern (like *.cpp and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01000}01000 \# *.h) to filter out the source-\/files in the directories. If left blank all}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01001}01001 \# files are included.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01002}01002 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01003}01003 EXAMPLE\_PATTERNS       = *}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01004}01004 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01005}01005 \# If the EXAMPLE\_RECURSIVE tag is set to YES then subdirectories will be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01006}01006 \# searched for input files to be used with the \(\backslash\)include or \(\backslash\)dontinclude commands}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01007}01007 \# irrespective of the value of the RECURSIVE tag.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01008}01008 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01009}01009 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01010}01010 EXAMPLE\_RECURSIVE      = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01011}01011 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01012}01012 \# The IMAGE\_PATH tag can be used to specify one or more files or directories}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01013}01013 \# that contain images that are to be included in the documentation (see the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01014}01014 \# \(\backslash\)image command).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01015}01015 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01016}01016 IMAGE\_PATH             =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01017}01017 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01018}01018 \# The INPUT\_FILTER tag can be used to specify a program that doxygen should}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01019}01019 \# invoke to filter for each input file. Doxygen will invoke the filter program}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01020}01020 \# by executing (via popen()) the command:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01021}01021 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01022}01022 \# <filter> <input-\/file>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01023}01023 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01024}01024 \# where <filter> is the value of the INPUT\_FILTER tag, and <input-\/file> is the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01025}01025 \# name of an input file. Doxygen will then use the output that the filter}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01026}01026 \# program writes to standard output. If FILTER\_PATTERNS is specified, this tag}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01027}01027 \# will be ignored.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01028}01028 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01029}01029 \# Note that the filter must not add or remove lines; it is applied before the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01030}01030 \# code is scanned, but not when the output code is generated. If lines are added}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01031}01031 \# or removed, the anchors will not be placed correctly.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01032}01032 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01033}01033 \# Note that for custom extensions or not directly supported extensions you also}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01034}01034 \# need to set EXTENSION\_MAPPING for the extension otherwise the files are not}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01035}01035 \# properly processed by doxygen.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01036}01036 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01037}01037 INPUT\_FILTER           =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01038}01038 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01039}01039 \# The FILTER\_PATTERNS tag can be used to specify filters on a per file pattern}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01040}01040 \# basis. Doxygen will compare the file name with each pattern and apply the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01041}01041 \# filter if there is a match. The filters are a list of the form: pattern=filter}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01042}01042 \# (like *.cpp=my\_cpp\_filter). See INPUT\_FILTER for further information on how}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01043}01043 \# filters are used. If the FILTER\_PATTERNS tag is empty or if none of the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01044}01044 \# patterns match the file name, INPUT\_FILTER is applied.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01045}01045 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01046}01046 \# Note that for custom extensions or not directly supported extensions you also}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01047}01047 \# need to set EXTENSION\_MAPPING for the extension otherwise the files are not}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01048}01048 \# properly processed by doxygen.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01049}01049 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01050}01050 FILTER\_PATTERNS        =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01051}01051 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01052}01052 \# If the FILTER\_SOURCE\_FILES tag is set to YES, the input filter (if set using}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01053}01053 \# INPUT\_FILTER) will also be used to filter the input files that are used for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01054}01054 \# producing the source files to browse (i.e. when SOURCE\_BROWSER is set to YES).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01055}01055 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01056}01056 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01057}01057 FILTER\_SOURCE\_FILES    = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01058}01058 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01059}01059 \# The FILTER\_SOURCE\_PATTERNS tag can be used to specify source filters per file}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01060}01060 \# pattern. A pattern will override the setting for FILTER\_PATTERN (if any) and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01061}01061 \# it is also possible to disable source filtering for a specific pattern using}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01062}01062 \# *.ext= (so without naming a filter).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01063}01063 \# This tag requires that the tag FILTER\_SOURCE\_FILES is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01064}01064 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01065}01065 FILTER\_SOURCE\_PATTERNS =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01066}01066 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01067}01067 \# If the USE\_MDFILE\_AS\_MAINPAGE tag refers to the name of a markdown file that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01068}01068 \# is part of the input, its contents will be placed on the main page}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01069}01069 \# (index.html). This can be useful if you have a project on for instance GitHub}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01070}01070 \# and want to reuse the introduction page also for the doxygen output.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01071}01071 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01072}01072 USE\_MDFILE\_AS\_MAINPAGE =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01073}01073 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01075}01075 \# Configuration options related to source browsing}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01076}01076 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01077}01077 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01078}01078 \# If the SOURCE\_BROWSER tag is set to YES then a list of source files will be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01079}01079 \# generated. Documented entities will be cross-\/referenced with these sources.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01080}01080 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01081}01081 \# Note: To get rid of all source code in the generated output, make sure that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01082}01082 \# also VERBATIM\_HEADERS is set to NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01083}01083 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01084}01084 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01085}01085 SOURCE\_BROWSER         = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01086}01086 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01087}01087 \# Setting the INLINE\_SOURCES tag to YES will include the body of functions,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01088}01088 \# classes and enums directly into the documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01089}01089 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01090}01090 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01091}01091 INLINE\_SOURCES         = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01092}01092 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01093}01093 \# Setting the STRIP\_CODE\_COMMENTS tag to YES will instruct doxygen to hide any}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01094}01094 \# special comment blocks from generated source code fragments. Normal C, C++ and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01095}01095 \# Fortran comments will always remain visible.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01096}01096 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01097}01097 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01098}01098 STRIP\_CODE\_COMMENTS    = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01099}01099 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01100}01100 \# If the REFERENCED\_BY\_RELATION tag is set to YES then for each documented}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01101}01101 \# entity all documented functions referencing it will be listed.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01102}01102 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01103}01103 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01104}01104 REFERENCED\_BY\_RELATION = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01105}01105 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01106}01106 \# If the REFERENCES\_RELATION tag is set to YES then for each documented function}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01107}01107 \# all documented entities called/used by that function will be listed.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01108}01108 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01109}01109 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01110}01110 REFERENCES\_RELATION    = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01111}01111 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01112}01112 \# If the REFERENCES\_LINK\_SOURCE tag is set to YES and SOURCE\_BROWSER tag is set}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01113}01113 \# to YES then the hyperlinks from functions in REFERENCES\_RELATION and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01114}01114 \# REFERENCED\_BY\_RELATION lists will link to the source code. Otherwise they will}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01115}01115 \# link to the documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01116}01116 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01117}01117 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01118}01118 REFERENCES\_LINK\_SOURCE = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01119}01119 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01120}01120 \# If SOURCE\_TOOLTIPS is enabled (the default) then hovering a hyperlink in the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01121}01121 \# source code will show a tooltip with additional information such as prototype,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01122}01122 \# brief description and links to the definition and documentation. Since this}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01123}01123 \# will make the HTML file larger and loading of large files a bit slower, you}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01124}01124 \# can opt to disable this feature.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01125}01125 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01126}01126 \# This tag requires that the tag SOURCE\_BROWSER is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01127}01127 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01128}01128 SOURCE\_TOOLTIPS        = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01129}01129 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01130}01130 \# If the USE\_HTAGS tag is set to YES then the references to source code will}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01131}01131 \# point to the HTML generated by the htags(1) tool instead of doxygen built-\/in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01132}01132 \# source browser. The htags tool is part of GNU's global source tagging system}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01133}01133 \# (see https://www.gnu.org/software/global/global.html). You will need version}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01134}01134 \# 4.8.6 or higher.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01135}01135 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01136}01136 \# To use it do the following:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01137}01137 \# -\/ Install the latest version of global}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01138}01138 \# -\/ Enable SOURCE\_BROWSER and USE\_HTAGS in the configuration file}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01139}01139 \# -\/ Make sure the INPUT points to the root of the source tree}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01140}01140 \# -\/ Run doxygen as normal}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01141}01141 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01142}01142 \# Doxygen will invoke htags (and that will in turn invoke gtags), so these}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01143}01143 \# tools must be available from the command line (i.e. in the search path).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01144}01144 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01145}01145 \# The result: instead of the source browser generated by doxygen, the links to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01146}01146 \# source code will now point to the output of htags.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01147}01147 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01148}01148 \# This tag requires that the tag SOURCE\_BROWSER is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01149}01149 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01150}01150 USE\_HTAGS              = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01151}01151 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01152}01152 \# If the VERBATIM\_HEADERS tag is set the YES then doxygen will generate a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01153}01153 \# verbatim copy of the header file for each class for which an include is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01154}01154 \# specified. Set to NO to disable this.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01155}01155 \# See also: Section \(\backslash\)class.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01156}01156 \# The default value is: YES.}
