\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01161}01161 \# Configuration options related to the alphabetical class index}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01162}01162 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01163}01163 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01164}01164 \# If the ALPHABETICAL\_INDEX tag is set to YES, an alphabetical index of all}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01165}01165 \# compounds will be generated. Enable this if the project contains a lot of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01166}01166 \# classes, structs, unions or interfaces.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01167}01167 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01168}01168 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01169}01169 ALPHABETICAL\_INDEX     = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01170}01170 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01171}01171 \# In case all classes in a project start with a common prefix, all classes will}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01172}01172 \# be put under the same header in the alphabetical index. The IGNORE\_PREFIX tag}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01173}01173 \# can be used to specify a prefix (or a list of prefixes) that should be ignored}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01174}01174 \# while generating the index headers.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01175}01175 \# This tag requires that the tag ALPHABETICAL\_INDEX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01176}01176 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01177}01177 IGNORE\_PREFIX          =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01178}01178 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01179}01179 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01180}01180 \# Configuration options related to the HTML output}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01181}01181 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01182}01182 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01183}01183 \# If the GENERATE\_HTML tag is set to YES, doxygen will generate HTML output}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01184}01184 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01185}01185 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01186}01186 GENERATE\_HTML          = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01187}01187 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01188}01188 \# The HTML\_OUTPUT tag is used to specify where the HTML docs will be put. If a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01189}01189 \# relative path is entered the value of OUTPUT\_DIRECTORY will be put in front of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01190}01190 \# it.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01191}01191 \# The default directory is: html.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01192}01192 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01193}01193 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01194}01194 HTML\_OUTPUT            = html}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01195}01195 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01196}01196 \# The HTML\_FILE\_EXTENSION tag can be used to specify the file extension for each}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01197}01197 \# generated HTML page (for example: .htm, .php, .asp).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01198}01198 \# The default value is: .html.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01199}01199 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01200}01200 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01201}01201 HTML\_FILE\_EXTENSION    = .html}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01202}01202 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01203}01203 \# The HTML\_HEADER tag can be used to specify a user-\/defined HTML header file for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01204}01204 \# each generated HTML page. If the tag is left blank doxygen will generate a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01205}01205 \# standard header.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01206}01206 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01207}01207 \# To get valid HTML the header file that includes any scripts and style sheets}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01208}01208 \# that doxygen needs, which is dependent on the configuration options used (e.g.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01209}01209 \# the setting GENERATE\_TREEVIEW). It is highly recommended to start with a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01210}01210 \# default header using}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01211}01211 \# doxygen -\/w html new\_header.html new\_footer.html new\_stylesheet.css}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01212}01212 \# YourConfigFile}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01213}01213 \# and then modify the file new\_header.html. See also section "{}Doxygen usage"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01214}01214 \# for information on how to generate the default header that doxygen normally}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01215}01215 \# uses.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01216}01216 \# Note: The header is subject to change so you typically have to regenerate the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01217}01217 \# default header when upgrading to a newer version of doxygen. For a description}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01218}01218 \# of the possible markers and block names see the documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01219}01219 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01220}01220 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01221}01221 HTML\_HEADER            =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01222}01222 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01223}01223 \# The HTML\_FOOTER tag can be used to specify a user-\/defined HTML footer for each}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01224}01224 \# generated HTML page. If the tag is left blank doxygen will generate a standard}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01225}01225 \# footer. See HTML\_HEADER for more information on how to generate a default}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01226}01226 \# footer and what special commands can be used inside the footer. See also}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01227}01227 \# section "{}Doxygen usage"{} for information on how to generate the default footer}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01228}01228 \# that doxygen normally uses.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01229}01229 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01230}01230 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01231}01231 HTML\_FOOTER            =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01232}01232 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01233}01233 \# The HTML\_STYLESHEET tag can be used to specify a user-\/defined cascading style}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01234}01234 \# sheet that is used by each HTML page. It can be used to fine-\/tune the look of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01235}01235 \# the HTML output. If left blank doxygen will generate a default style sheet.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01236}01236 \# See also section "{}Doxygen usage"{} for information on how to generate the style}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01237}01237 \# sheet that doxygen normally uses.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01238}01238 \# Note: It is recommended to use HTML\_EXTRA\_STYLESHEET instead of this tag, as}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01239}01239 \# it is more robust and this tag (HTML\_STYLESHEET) will in the future become}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01240}01240 \# obsolete.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01241}01241 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01242}01242 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01243}01243 HTML\_STYLESHEET        =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01244}01244 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01245}01245 \# The HTML\_EXTRA\_STYLESHEET tag can be used to specify additional user-\/defined}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01246}01246 \# cascading style sheets that are included after the standard style sheets}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01247}01247 \# created by doxygen. Using this option one can overrule certain style aspects.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01248}01248 \# This is preferred over using HTML\_STYLESHEET since it does not replace the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01249}01249 \# standard style sheet and is therefore more robust against future updates.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01250}01250 \# Doxygen will copy the style sheet files to the output directory.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01251}01251 \# Note: The order of the extra style sheet files is of importance (e.g. the last}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01252}01252 \# style sheet in the list overrules the setting of the previous ones in the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01253}01253 \# list). For an example see the documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01254}01254 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01255}01255 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01256}01256 HTML\_EXTRA\_STYLESHEET  =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01257}01257 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01258}01258 \# The HTML\_EXTRA\_FILES tag can be used to specify one or more extra images or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01259}01259 \# other source files which should be copied to the HTML output directory. Note}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01260}01260 \# that these files will be copied to the base HTML output directory. Use the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01261}01261 \# \$relpath\string^ marker in the HTML\_HEADER and/or HTML\_FOOTER files to load these}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01262}01262 \# files. In the HTML\_STYLESHEET file, use the file name only. Also note that the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01263}01263 \# files will be copied as-\/is; there are no commands or markers available.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01264}01264 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01265}01265 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01266}01266 HTML\_EXTRA\_FILES       =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01267}01267 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01268}01268 \# The HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_HUE tag controls the color of the HTML output. Doxygen}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01269}01269 \# will adjust the colors in the style sheet and background images according to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01270}01270 \# this color. Hue is specified as an angle on a color-\/wheel, see}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01271}01271 \# https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hue for more information. For instance the value}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01272}01272 \# 0 represents red, 60 is yellow, 120 is green, 180 is cyan, 240 is blue, 300}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01273}01273 \# purple, and 360 is red again.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01274}01274 \# Minimum value: 0, maximum value: 359, default value: 220.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01275}01275 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01276}01276 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01277}01277 HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_HUE    = 220}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01278}01278 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01279}01279 \# The HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_SAT tag controls the purity (or saturation) of the colors}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01280}01280 \# in the HTML output. For a value of 0 the output will use gray-\/scales only. A}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01281}01281 \# value of 255 will produce the most vivid colors.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01282}01282 \# Minimum value: 0, maximum value: 255, default value: 100.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01283}01283 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01284}01284 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01285}01285 HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_SAT    = 100}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01286}01286 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01287}01287 \# The HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_GAMMA tag controls the gamma correction applied to the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01288}01288 \# luminance component of the colors in the HTML output. Values below 100}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01289}01289 \# gradually make the output lighter, whereas values above 100 make the output}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01290}01290 \# darker. The value divided by 100 is the actual gamma applied, so 80 represents}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01291}01291 \# a gamma of 0.8, The value 220 represents a gamma of 2.2, and 100 does not}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01292}01292 \# change the gamma.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01293}01293 \# Minimum value: 40, maximum value: 240, default value: 80.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01294}01294 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01295}01295 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01296}01296 HTML\_COLORSTYLE\_GAMMA  = 80}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01297}01297 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01298}01298 \# If the HTML\_TIMESTAMP tag is set to YES then the footer of each generated HTML}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01299}01299 \# page will contain the date and time when the page was generated. Setting this}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01300}01300 \# to YES can help to show when doxygen was last run and thus if the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01301}01301 \# documentation is up to date.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01302}01302 \# The default value is: NO.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01307}01307 \# If the HTML\_DYNAMIC\_MENUS tag is set to YES then the generated HTML}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01308}01308 \# documentation will contain a main index with vertical navigation menus that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01309}01309 \# are dynamically created via JavaScript. If disabled, the navigation index will}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01310}01310 \# consists of multiple levels of tabs that are statically embedded in every HTML}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01311}01311 \# page. Disable this option to support browsers that do not have JavaScript,}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01312}01312 \# like the Qt help browser.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01313}01313 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01314}01314 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01315}01315 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01316}01316 HTML\_DYNAMIC\_MENUS     = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01317}01317 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01318}01318 \# If the HTML\_DYNAMIC\_SECTIONS tag is set to YES then the generated HTML}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01319}01319 \# documentation will contain sections that can be hidden and shown after the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01320}01320 \# page has loaded.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01324}01324 HTML\_DYNAMIC\_SECTIONS  = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01325}01325 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01326}01326 \# With HTML\_INDEX\_NUM\_ENTRIES one can control the preferred number of entries}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01327}01327 \# shown in the various tree structured indices initially; the user can expand}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01328}01328 \# and collapse entries dynamically later on. Doxygen will expand the tree to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01329}01329 \# such a level that at most the specified number of entries are visible (unless}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01330}01330 \# a fully collapsed tree already exceeds this amount). So setting the number of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01331}01331 \# entries 1 will produce a full collapsed tree by default. 0 is a special value}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01332}01332 \# representing an infinite number of entries and will result in a full expanded}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01333}01333 \# tree by default.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01334}01334 \# Minimum value: 0, maximum value: 9999, default value: 100.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01335}01335 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01336}01336 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01339}01339 \# If the GENERATE\_DOCSET tag is set to YES, additional index files will be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01340}01340 \# generated that can be used as input for Apple's Xcode 3 integrated development}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01341}01341 \# environment (see:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01342}01342 \# https://developer.apple.com/xcode/), introduced with OSX 10.5 (Leopard). To}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01343}01343 \# create a documentation set, doxygen will generate a Makefile in the HTML}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01344}01344 \# output directory. Running make will produce the docset in that directory and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01345}01345 \# running make install will install the docset in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01346}01346 \# \string~/Library/Developer/Shared/Documentation/DocSets so that Xcode will find it at}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01347}01347 \# startup. See https://developer.apple.com/library/archive/featuredarticles/Doxy}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01348}01348 \# genXcode/\_index.html for more information.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01349}01349 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01350}01350 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01351}01351 }

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01353}01353 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01354}01354 \# This tag determines the name of the docset feed. A documentation feed provides}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01384}01384 \# If the GENERATE\_HTMLHELP tag is set to YES then doxygen generates three}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01385}01385 \# additional HTML index files: index.hhp, index.hhc, and index.hhk. The}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01386}01386 \# index.hhp is a project file that can be read by Microsoft's HTML Help Workshop}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01387}01387 \# on Windows. In the beginning of 2021 Microsoft took the original page, with}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01388}01388 \# a.o. the download links, offline the HTML help workshop was already many years}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01389}01389 \# in maintenance mode). You can download the HTML help workshop from the web}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01390}01390 \# archives at Installation executable (see:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01391}01391 \# http://web.archive.org/web/20160201063255/http://download.microsoft.com/downlo}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01392}01392 \# ad/0/A/9/0A939EF6-\/E31C-\/430F-\/A3DF-\/DFAE7960D564/htmlhelp.exe).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01393}01393 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01394}01394 \# The HTML Help Workshop contains a compiler that can convert all HTML output}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01395}01395 \# generated by doxygen into a single compiled HTML file (.chm). Compiled HTML}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01396}01396 \# files are now used as the Windows 98 help format, and will replace the old}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01397}01397 \# Windows help format (.hlp) on all Windows platforms in the future. Compressed}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01398}01398 \# HTML files also contain an index, a table of contents, and you can search for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01399}01399 \# words in the documentation. The HTML workshop also contains a viewer for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01400}01400 \# compressed HTML files.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01401}01401 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01402}01402 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01403}01403 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01404}01404 GENERATE\_HTMLHELP      = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01405}01405 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01406}01406 \# The CHM\_FILE tag can be used to specify the file name of the resulting .chm}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01407}01407 \# file. You can add a path in front of the file if the result should not be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01408}01408 \# written to the html output directory.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01413}01413 \# The HHC\_LOCATION tag can be used to specify the location (absolute path}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01448}01448 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01449}01449 \# If the GENERATE\_QHP tag is set to YES and both QHP\_NAMESPACE and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01450}01450 \# QHP\_VIRTUAL\_FOLDER are set, an additional index file will be generated that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01451}01451 \# can be used as input for Qt's qhelpgenerator to generate a Qt Compressed Help}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01452}01452 \# (.qch) of the generated HTML documentation.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01454}01454 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01455}01455 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01456}01456 GENERATE\_QHP           = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01457}01457 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01458}01458 \# If the QHG\_LOCATION tag is specified, the QCH\_FILE tag can be used to specify}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01459}01459 \# the file name of the resulting .qch file. The path specified is relative to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01460}01460 \# the HTML output folder.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01461}01461 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_QHP is set to YES.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01506}01506 \# The QHG\_LOCATION tag can be used to specify the location (absolute path}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01507}01507 \# including file name) of Qt's qhelpgenerator. If non-\/empty doxygen will try to}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01511}01511 QHG\_LOCATION           =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01512}01512 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01513}01513 \# If the GENERATE\_ECLIPSEHELP tag is set to YES, additional index files will be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01514}01514 \# generated, together with the HTML files, they form an Eclipse help plugin. To}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01515}01515 \# install this plugin and make it available under the help contents menu in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01516}01516 \# Eclipse, the contents of the directory containing the HTML and XML files needs}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01517}01517 \# to be copied into the plugins directory of eclipse. The name of the directory}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01518}01518 \# within the plugins directory should be the same as the ECLIPSE\_DOC\_ID value.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01519}01519 \# After copying Eclipse needs to be restarted before the help appears.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01520}01520 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01521}01521 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01522}01522 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01523}01523 GENERATE\_ECLIPSEHELP   = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01524}01524 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01525}01525 \# A unique identifier for the Eclipse help plugin. When installing the plugin}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01526}01526 \# the directory name containing the HTML and XML files should also have this}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01527}01527 \# name. Each documentation set should have its own identifier.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01528}01528 \# The default value is: org.doxygen.Project.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01529}01529 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_ECLIPSEHELP is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01530}01530 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01531}01531 ECLIPSE\_DOC\_ID         = org.doxygen.Project}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01532}01532 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01533}01533 \# If you want full control over the layout of the generated HTML pages it might}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01534}01534 \# be necessary to disable the index and replace it with your own. The}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01535}01535 \# DISABLE\_INDEX tag can be used to turn on/off the condensed index (tabs) at top}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01536}01536 \# of each HTML page. A value of NO enables the index and the value YES disables}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01537}01537 \# it. Since the tabs in the index contain the same information as the navigation}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01538}01538 \# tree, you can set this option to YES if you also set GENERATE\_TREEVIEW to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01539}01539 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01540}01540 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01541}01541 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01542}01542 DISABLE\_INDEX          = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01543}01543 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01544}01544 \# The GENERATE\_TREEVIEW tag is used to specify whether a tree-\/like index}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01545}01545 \# structure should be generated to display hierarchical information. If the tag}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01546}01546 \# value is set to YES, a side panel will be generated containing a tree-\/like}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01547}01547 \# index structure (just like the one that is generated for HTML Help). For this}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01548}01548 \# to work a browser that supports JavaScript, DHTML, CSS and frames is required}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01549}01549 \# (i.e. any modern browser). Windows users are probably better off using the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01550}01550 \# HTML help feature. Via custom style sheets (see HTML\_EXTRA\_STYLESHEET) one can}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01551}01551 \# further fine tune the look of the index (see "{}Fine-\/tuning the output"{}). As an}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01552}01552 \# example, the default style sheet generated by doxygen has an example that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01553}01553 \# shows how to put an image at the root of the tree instead of the PROJECT\_NAME.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01554}01554 \# Since the tree basically has the same information as the tab index, you could}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01555}01555 \# consider setting DISABLE\_INDEX to YES when enabling this option.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01556}01556 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01557}01557 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01558}01558 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01559}01559 GENERATE\_TREEVIEW      = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01560}01560 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01561}01561 \# When both GENERATE\_TREEVIEW and DISABLE\_INDEX are set to YES, then the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01562}01562 \# FULL\_SIDEBAR option determines if the side bar is limited to only the treeview}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01563}01563 \# area (value NO) or if it should extend to the full height of the window (value}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01564}01564 \# YES). Setting this to YES gives a layout similar to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01565}01565 \# https://docs.readthedocs.io with more room for contents, but less room for the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01566}01566 \# project logo, title, and description. If either GENERATOR\_TREEVIEW or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01567}01567 \# DISABLE\_INDEX is set to NO, this option has no effect.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01568}01568 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01569}01569 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01570}01570 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01571}01571 FULL\_SIDEBAR           = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01572}01572 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01573}01573 \# The ENUM\_VALUES\_PER\_LINE tag can be used to set the number of enum values that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01574}01574 \# doxygen will group on one line in the generated HTML documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01575}01575 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01576}01576 \# Note that a value of 0 will completely suppress the enum values from appearing}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01577}01577 \# in the overview section.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01578}01578 \# Minimum value: 0, maximum value: 20, default value: 4.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01579}01579 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01580}01580 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01581}01581 ENUM\_VALUES\_PER\_LINE   = 4}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01582}01582 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01583}01583 \# If the treeview is enabled (see GENERATE\_TREEVIEW) then this tag can be used}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01584}01584 \# to set the initial width (in pixels) of the frame in which the tree is shown.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01588}01588 TREEVIEW\_WIDTH         = 250}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01589}01589 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01590}01590 \# If the EXT\_LINKS\_IN\_WINDOW option is set to YES, doxygen will open links to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01591}01591 \# external symbols imported via tag files in a separate window.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01595}01595 EXT\_LINKS\_IN\_WINDOW    = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01596}01596 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01597}01597 \# If the HTML\_FORMULA\_FORMAT option is set to svg, doxygen will use the pdf2svg}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01598}01598 \# tool (see https://github.com/dawbarton/pdf2svg) or inkscape (see}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01599}01599 \# https://inkscape.org) to generate formulas as SVG images instead of PNGs for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01600}01600 \# the HTML output. These images will generally look nicer at scaled resolutions.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01601}01601 \# Possible values are: png (the default) and svg (looks nicer but requires the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01602}01602 \# pdf2svg or inkscape tool).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01603}01603 \# The default value is: png.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01604}01604 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01605}01605 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01606}01606 HTML\_FORMULA\_FORMAT    = png}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01607}01607 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01608}01608 \# Use this tag to change the font size of LaTeX formulas included as images in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01609}01609 \# the HTML documentation. When you change the font size after a successful}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01610}01610 \# doxygen run you need to manually remove any form\_*.png images from the HTML}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01611}01611 \# output directory to force them to be regenerated.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01612}01612 \# Minimum value: 8, maximum value: 50, default value: 10.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01613}01613 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01614}01614 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01615}01615 FORMULA\_FONTSIZE       = 10}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01616}01616 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01617}01617 \# Use the FORMULA\_TRANSPARENT tag to determine whether or not the images}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01618}01618 \# generated for formulas are transparent PNGs. Transparent PNGs are not}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01619}01619 \# supported properly for IE 6.0, but are supported on all modern browsers.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01620}01620 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01621}01621 \# Note that when changing this option you need to delete any form\_*.png files in}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01622}01622 \# the HTML output directory before the changes have effect.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01623}01623 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01624}01624 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01625}01625 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01626}01626 FORMULA\_TRANSPARENT    = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01627}01627 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01628}01628 \# The FORMULA\_MACROFILE can contain LaTeX \(\backslash\)newcommand and \(\backslash\)renewcommand commands}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01629}01629 \# to create new LaTeX commands to be used in formulas as building blocks. See}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01630}01630 \# the section "{}Including formulas"{} for details.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01632}01632 FORMULA\_MACROFILE      =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01633}01633 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01634}01634 \# Enable the USE\_MATHJAX option to render LaTeX formulas using MathJax (see}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01635}01635 \# https://www.mathjax.org) which uses client side JavaScript for the rendering}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01636}01636 \# instead of using pre-\/rendered bitmaps. Use this if you do not have LaTeX}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01637}01637 \# installed or if you want to formulas look prettier in the HTML output. When}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01638}01638 \# enabled you may also need to install MathJax separately and configure the path}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01639}01639 \# to it using the MATHJAX\_RELPATH option.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01640}01640 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01641}01641 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01642}01642 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01643}01643 USE\_MATHJAX            = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01644}01644 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01645}01645 \# With MATHJAX\_VERSION it is possible to specify the MathJax version to be used.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01646}01646 \# Note that the different versions of MathJax have different requirements with}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01647}01647 \# regards to the different settings, so it is possible that also other MathJax}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01648}01648 \# settings have to be changed when switching between the different MathJax}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01649}01649 \# versions.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01650}01650 \# Possible values are: MathJax\_2 and MathJax\_3.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01651}01651 \# The default value is: MathJax\_2.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01652}01652 \# This tag requires that the tag USE\_MATHJAX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01653}01653 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01654}01654 MATHJAX\_VERSION        = MathJax\_2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01655}01655 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01656}01656 \# When MathJax is enabled you can set the default output format to be used for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01657}01657 \# the MathJax output. For more details about the output format see MathJax}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01658}01658 \# version 2 (see:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01659}01659 \# http://docs.mathjax.org/en/v2.7-\/latest/output.html) and MathJax version 3}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01660}01660 \# (see:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01661}01661 \# http://docs.mathjax.org/en/latest/web/components/output.html).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01662}01662 \# Possible values are: HTML-\/CSS (which is slower, but has the best}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01663}01663 \# compatibility. This is the name for Mathjax version 2, for MathJax version 3}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01664}01664 \# this will be translated into chtml), NativeMML (i.e. MathML. Only supported}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01665}01665 \# for NathJax 2. For MathJax version 3 chtml will be used instead.), chtml (This}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01666}01666 \# is the name for Mathjax version 3, for MathJax version 2 this will be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01667}01667 \# translated into HTML-\/CSS) and SVG.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01668}01668 \# The default value is: HTML-\/CSS.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01669}01669 \# This tag requires that the tag USE\_MATHJAX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01670}01670 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01671}01671 MATHJAX\_FORMAT         = HTML-\/CSS}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01672}01672 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01673}01673 \# When MathJax is enabled you need to specify the location relative to the HTML}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01674}01674 \# output directory using the MATHJAX\_RELPATH option. The destination directory}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01675}01675 \# should contain the MathJax.js script. For instance, if the mathjax directory}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01676}01676 \# is located at the same level as the HTML output directory, then}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01677}01677 \# MATHJAX\_RELPATH should be ../mathjax. The default value points to the MathJax}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01678}01678 \# Content Delivery Network so you can quickly see the result without installing}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01679}01679 \# MathJax. However, it is strongly recommended to install a local copy of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01680}01680 \# MathJax from https://www.mathjax.org before deployment. The default value is:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01681}01681 \# -\/ in case of MathJax version 2: https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/mathjax@2}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01682}01682 \# -\/ in case of MathJax version 3: https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/npm/mathjax@3}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01683}01683 \# This tag requires that the tag USE\_MATHJAX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01684}01684 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01685}01685 MATHJAX\_RELPATH        =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01686}01686 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01687}01687 \# The MATHJAX\_EXTENSIONS tag can be used to specify one or more MathJax}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01688}01688 \# extension names that should be enabled during MathJax rendering. For example}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01689}01689 \# for MathJax version 2 (see https://docs.mathjax.org/en/v2.7-\/latest/tex.html}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01690}01690 \# \#tex-\/and-\/latex-\/extensions):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01691}01691 \# MATHJAX\_EXTENSIONS = TeX/AMSmath TeX/AMSsymbols}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01692}01692 \# For example for MathJax version 3 (see}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01693}01693 \# http://docs.mathjax.org/en/latest/input/tex/extensions/index.html):}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01694}01694 \# MATHJAX\_EXTENSIONS = ams}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01695}01695 \# This tag requires that the tag USE\_MATHJAX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01696}01696 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01697}01697 MATHJAX\_EXTENSIONS     =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01698}01698 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01699}01699 \# The MATHJAX\_CODEFILE tag can be used to specify a file with javascript pieces}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01700}01700 \# of code that will be used on startup of the MathJax code. See the MathJax site}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01701}01701 \# (see:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01702}01702 \# http://docs.mathjax.org/en/v2.7-\/latest/output.html) for more details. For an}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01703}01703 \# example see the documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01704}01704 \# This tag requires that the tag USE\_MATHJAX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01705}01705 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01706}01706 MATHJAX\_CODEFILE       =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01707}01707 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01708}01708 \# When the SEARCHENGINE tag is enabled doxygen will generate a search box for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01709}01709 \# the HTML output. The underlying search engine uses javascript and DHTML and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01710}01710 \# should work on any modern browser. Note that when using HTML help}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01711}01711 \# (GENERATE\_HTMLHELP), Qt help (GENERATE\_QHP), or docsets (GENERATE\_DOCSET)}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01712}01712 \# there is already a search function so this one should typically be disabled.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01713}01713 \# For large projects the javascript based search engine can be slow, then}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01714}01714 \# enabling SERVER\_BASED\_SEARCH may provide a better solution. It is possible to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01715}01715 \# search using the keyboard; to jump to the search box use <access key> + S}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01716}01716 \# (what the <access key> is depends on the OS and browser, but it is typically}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01717}01717 \# <CTRL>, <ALT>/<option>, or both). Inside the search box use the <cursor down}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01718}01718 \# key> to jump into the search results window, the results can be navigated}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01719}01719 \# using the <cursor keys>. Press <Enter> to select an item or <escape> to cancel}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01720}01720 \# the search. The filter options can be selected when the cursor is inside the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01721}01721 \# search box by pressing <Shift>+<cursor down>. Also here use the <cursor keys>}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01722}01722 \# to select a filter and <Enter> or <escape> to activate or cancel the filter}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01723}01723 \# option.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01724}01724 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01725}01725 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_HTML is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01726}01726 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01727}01727 SEARCHENGINE           = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01728}01728 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01729}01729 \# When the SERVER\_BASED\_SEARCH tag is enabled the search engine will be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01730}01730 \# implemented using a web server instead of a web client using JavaScript. There}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01731}01731 \# are two flavors of web server based searching depending on the EXTERNAL\_SEARCH}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01732}01732 \# setting. When disabled, doxygen will generate a PHP script for searching and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01733}01733 \# an index file used by the script. When EXTERNAL\_SEARCH is enabled the indexing}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01734}01734 \# and searching needs to be provided by external tools. See the section}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01735}01735 \# "{}External Indexing and Searching"{} for details.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01736}01736 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01737}01737 \# This tag requires that the tag SEARCHENGINE is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01738}01738 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01739}01739 SERVER\_BASED\_SEARCH    = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01740}01740 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01741}01741 \# When EXTERNAL\_SEARCH tag is enabled doxygen will no longer generate the PHP}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01742}01742 \# script for searching. Instead the search results are written to an XML file}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01743}01743 \# which needs to be processed by an external indexer. Doxygen will invoke an}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01744}01744 \# external search engine pointed to by the SEARCHENGINE\_URL option to obtain the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01745}01745 \# search results.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01746}01746 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01747}01747 \# Doxygen ships with an example indexer (doxyindexer) and search engine}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01748}01748 \# (doxysearch.cgi) which are based on the open source search engine library}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01749}01749 \# Xapian (see:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01750}01750 \# https://xapian.org/).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01751}01751 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01752}01752 \# See the section "{}External Indexing and Searching"{} for details.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01753}01753 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01754}01754 \# This tag requires that the tag SEARCHENGINE is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01755}01755 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01756}01756 EXTERNAL\_SEARCH        = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01757}01757 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01758}01758 \# The SEARCHENGINE\_URL should point to a search engine hosted by a web server}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01759}01759 \# which will return the search results when EXTERNAL\_SEARCH is enabled.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01760}01760 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01761}01761 \# Doxygen ships with an example indexer (doxyindexer) and search engine}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01762}01762 \# (doxysearch.cgi) which are based on the open source search engine library}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01763}01763 \# Xapian (see:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01764}01764 \# https://xapian.org/). See the section "{}External Indexing and Searching"{} for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01765}01765 \# details.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01766}01766 \# This tag requires that the tag SEARCHENGINE is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01767}01767 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01768}01768 SEARCHENGINE\_URL       =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01769}01769 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01770}01770 \# When SERVER\_BASED\_SEARCH and EXTERNAL\_SEARCH are both enabled the unindexed}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01771}01771 \# search data is written to a file for indexing by an external tool. With the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01772}01772 \# SEARCHDATA\_FILE tag the name of this file can be specified.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01773}01773 \# The default file is: searchdata.xml.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01774}01774 \# This tag requires that the tag SEARCHENGINE is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01775}01775 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01776}01776 SEARCHDATA\_FILE        = searchdata.xml}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01777}01777 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01778}01778 \# When SERVER\_BASED\_SEARCH and EXTERNAL\_SEARCH are both enabled the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01779}01779 \# EXTERNAL\_SEARCH\_ID tag can be used as an identifier for the project. This is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01780}01780 \# useful in combination with EXTRA\_SEARCH\_MAPPINGS to search through multiple}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01781}01781 \# projects and redirect the results back to the right project.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01782}01782 \# This tag requires that the tag SEARCHENGINE is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01783}01783 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01784}01784 EXTERNAL\_SEARCH\_ID     =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01785}01785 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01786}01786 \# The EXTRA\_SEARCH\_MAPPINGS tag can be used to enable searching through doxygen}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01787}01787 \# projects other than the one defined by this configuration file, but that are}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01788}01788 \# all added to the same external search index. Each project needs to have a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01789}01789 \# unique id set via EXTERNAL\_SEARCH\_ID. The search mapping then maps the id of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01790}01790 \# to a relative location where the documentation can be found. The format is:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01791}01791 \# EXTRA\_SEARCH\_MAPPINGS = tagname1=loc1 tagname2=loc2 ...}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01792}01792 \# This tag requires that the tag SEARCHENGINE is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01793}01793 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01794}01794 EXTRA\_SEARCH\_MAPPINGS  =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01795}01795 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01796}01796 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01797}01797 \# Configuration options related to the LaTeX output}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01798}01798 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01799}01799 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01800}01800 \# If the GENERATE\_LATEX tag is set to YES, doxygen will generate LaTeX output.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01801}01801 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01802}01802 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01803}01803 GENERATE\_LATEX         = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01804}01804 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01805}01805 \# The LATEX\_OUTPUT tag is used to specify where the LaTeX docs will be put. If a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01806}01806 \# relative path is entered the value of OUTPUT\_DIRECTORY will be put in front of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01807}01807 \# it.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01808}01808 \# The default directory is: latex.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01809}01809 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_LATEX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01810}01810 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01811}01811 LATEX\_OUTPUT           = latex}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01812}01812 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01813}01813 \# The LATEX\_CMD\_NAME tag can be used to specify the LaTeX command name to be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01814}01814 \# invoked.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01815}01815 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01816}01816 \# Note that when not enabling USE\_PDFLATEX the default is latex when enabling}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01817}01817 \# USE\_PDFLATEX the default is pdflatex and when in the later case latex is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01818}01818 \# chosen this is overwritten by pdflatex. For specific output languages the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01819}01819 \# default can have been set differently, this depends on the implementation of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01820}01820 \# the output language.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01821}01821 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_LATEX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01822}01822 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01823}01823 LATEX\_CMD\_NAME         =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01824}01824 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01825}01825 \# The MAKEINDEX\_CMD\_NAME tag can be used to specify the command name to generate}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01826}01826 \# index for LaTeX.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01827}01827 \# Note: This tag is used in the Makefile / make.bat.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01828}01828 \# See also: LATEX\_MAKEINDEX\_CMD for the part in the generated output file}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01829}01829 \# (.tex).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01830}01830 \# The default file is: makeindex.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01831}01831 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_LATEX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01832}01832 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01833}01833 MAKEINDEX\_CMD\_NAME     = makeindex}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01834}01834 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01835}01835 \# The LATEX\_MAKEINDEX\_CMD tag can be used to specify the command name to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01836}01836 \# generate index for LaTeX. In case there is no backslash (\(\backslash\)) as first character}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01837}01837 \# it will be automatically added in the LaTeX code.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01838}01838 \# Note: This tag is used in the generated output file (.tex).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01839}01839 \# See also: MAKEINDEX\_CMD\_NAME for the part in the Makefile / make.bat.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01840}01840 \# The default value is: makeindex.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01841}01841 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_LATEX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01842}01842 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01843}01843 LATEX\_MAKEINDEX\_CMD    = makeindex}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01844}01844 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01845}01845 \# If the COMPACT\_LATEX tag is set to YES, doxygen generates more compact LaTeX}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01846}01846 \# documents. This may be useful for small projects and may help to save some}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01847}01847 \# trees in general.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01848}01848 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01849}01849 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_LATEX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01850}01850 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01851}01851 COMPACT\_LATEX          = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01852}01852 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01853}01853 \# The PAPER\_TYPE tag can be used to set the paper type that is used by the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01854}01854 \# printer.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01855}01855 \# Possible values are: a4 (210 x 297 mm), letter (8.5 x 11 inches), legal (8.5 x}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01856}01856 \# 14 inches) and executive (7.25 x 10.5 inches).}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01857}01857 \# The default value is: a4.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01858}01858 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_LATEX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01859}01859 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01860}01860 PAPER\_TYPE             = a4}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01861}01861 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01862}01862 \# The EXTRA\_PACKAGES tag can be used to specify one or more LaTeX package names}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01863}01863 \# that should be included in the LaTeX output. The package can be specified just}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01864}01864 \# by its name or with the correct syntax as to be used with the LaTeX}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01865}01865 \# \(\backslash\)usepackage command. To get the times font for instance you can specify :}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01866}01866 \# EXTRA\_PACKAGES=times or EXTRA\_PACKAGES=\{times\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01867}01867 \# To use the option intlimits with the amsmath package you can specify:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01868}01868 \# EXTRA\_PACKAGES=[intlimits]\{amsmath\}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01869}01869 \# If left blank no extra packages will be included.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01870}01870 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_LATEX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01871}01871 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01872}01872 EXTRA\_PACKAGES         =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01873}01873 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01874}01874 \# The LATEX\_HEADER tag can be used to specify a user-\/defined LaTeX header for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01875}01875 \# the generated LaTeX document. The header should contain everything until the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01876}01876 \# first chapter. If it is left blank doxygen will generate a standard header. It}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01877}01877 \# is highly recommended to start with a default header using}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01878}01878 \# doxygen -\/w latex new\_header.tex new\_footer.tex new\_stylesheet.sty}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01879}01879 \# and then modify the file new\_header.tex. See also section "{}Doxygen usage"{} for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01880}01880 \# information on how to generate the default header that doxygen normally uses.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01881}01881 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01882}01882 \# Note: Only use a user-\/defined header if you know what you are doing!}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01883}01883 \# Note: The header is subject to change so you typically have to regenerate the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01884}01884 \# default header when upgrading to a newer version of doxygen. The following}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01885}01885 \# commands have a special meaning inside the header (and footer): For a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01886}01886 \# description of the possible markers and block names see the documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01887}01887 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_LATEX is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01888}01888 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01889}01889 LATEX\_HEADER           =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01890}01890 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01891}01891 \# The LATEX\_FOOTER tag can be used to specify a user-\/defined LaTeX footer for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01892}01892 \# the generated LaTeX document. The footer should contain everything after the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01893}01893 \# last chapter. If it is left blank doxygen will generate a standard footer. See}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01894}01894 \# LATEX\_HEADER for more information on how to generate a default footer and what}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01895}01895 \# special commands can be used inside the footer. See also section "{}Doxygen}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01896}01896 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# usage"{} for information on how to generate the default footer that doxygen}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01897}01897 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# normally uses. Note: Only use a user-\/defined footer if you know what you are}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01898}01898 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# doing!}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01899}01899 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_LATEX is set to YES.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01900}01900 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01903}01903 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The LATEX\_EXTRA\_STYLESHEET tag can be used to specify additional user-\/defined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01904}01904 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# LaTeX style sheets that are included after the standard style sheets created}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01906}01906 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# will copy the style sheet files to the output directory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01907}01907 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# Note: The order of the extra style sheet files is of importance (e.g. the last}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01910}01910 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_LATEX is set to YES.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01922}01922 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# If the PDF\_HYPERLINKS tag is set to YES, the LaTeX that is generated is}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01923}01923 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# prepared for conversion to PDF (using ps2pdf or pdflatex). The PDF file will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01924}01924 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# contain links (just like the HTML output) instead of page references. This}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01925}01925 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# makes the output suitable for online browsing using a PDF viewer.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01926}01926 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The default value is: YES.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01933}01933 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# files. Set this option to YES, to get a higher quality PDF documentation.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01982}01982 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
