\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01984}01984 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# If the GENERATE\_RTF tag is set to YES, doxygen will generate RTF output. The}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01985}01985 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# RTF output is optimized for Word 97 and may not look too pretty with other RTF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01986}01986 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# readers/editors.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01987}01987 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The default value is: NO.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01988}01988 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01989}01989 \textcolor{preprocessor}{GENERATE\_RTF           = NO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01990}01990 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01991}01991 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The RTF\_OUTPUT tag is used to specify where the RTF docs will be put. If a}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01992}01992 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# relative path is entered the value of OUTPUT\_DIRECTORY will be put in front of}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01993}01993 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# it.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01994}01994 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The default directory is: rtf.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01995}01995 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_RTF is set to YES.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01996}01996 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01997}01997 \textcolor{preprocessor}{RTF\_OUTPUT             = rtf}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01998}01998 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l01999}01999 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# If the COMPACT\_RTF tag is set to YES, doxygen generates more compact RTF}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02000}02000 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# documents. This may be useful for small projects and may help to save some}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02001}02001 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# trees in general.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02002}02002 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The default value is: NO.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02003}02003 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_RTF is set to YES.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02004}02004 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02005}02005 \textcolor{preprocessor}{COMPACT\_RTF            = NO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02006}02006 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02007}02007 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# If the RTF\_HYPERLINKS tag is set to YES, the RTF that is generated will}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02008}02008 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# contain hyperlink fields. The RTF file will contain links (just like the HTML}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02009}02009 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# output) instead of page references. This makes the output suitable for online}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02010}02010 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# browsing using Word or some other Word compatible readers that support those}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02011}02011 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# fields.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02012}02012 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02013}02013 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# Note: WordPad (write) and others do not support links.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02014}02014 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The default value is: NO.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02015}02015 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_RTF is set to YES.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02016}02016 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02018}02018 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02019}02019 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# Load stylesheet definitions from file. Syntax is similar to doxygen's}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02020}02020 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# configuration file, i.e. a series of assignments. You only have to provide}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02021}02021 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# replacements, missing definitions are set to their default value.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02022}02022 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02023}02023 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# See also section "{}}Doxygen usage"{} for information on how to generate the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02024}02024 \# default style sheet that doxygen normally uses.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02025}02025 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_RTF is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02026}02026 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02027}02027 RTF\_STYLESHEET\_FILE    =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02028}02028 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02029}02029 \# Set optional variables used in the generation of an RTF document. Syntax is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02030}02030 \# similar to doxygen's configuration file. A template extensions file can be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02031}02031 \# generated using doxygen -\/e rtf extensionFile.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02032}02032 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_RTF is set to YES.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02036}02036 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02037}02037 \# Configuration options related to the man page output}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02038}02038 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02039}02039 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02040}02040 \# If the GENERATE\_MAN tag is set to YES, doxygen will generate man pages for}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02041}02041 \# classes and files.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02042}02042 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02043}02043 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02044}02044 GENERATE\_MAN           = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02045}02045 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02046}02046 \# The MAN\_OUTPUT tag is used to specify where the man pages will be put. If a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02047}02047 \# relative path is entered the value of OUTPUT\_DIRECTORY will be put in front of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02048}02048 \# it. A directory man3 will be created inside the directory specified by}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02049}02049 \# MAN\_OUTPUT.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02050}02050 \# The default directory is: man.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02051}02051 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_MAN is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02052}02052 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02053}02053 MAN\_OUTPUT             = man}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02054}02054 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02055}02055 \# The MAN\_EXTENSION tag determines the extension that is added to the generated}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02056}02056 \# man pages. In case the manual section does not start with a number, the number}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02057}02057 \# 3 is prepended. The dot (.) at the beginning of the MAN\_EXTENSION tag is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02058}02058 \# optional.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02059}02059 \# The default value is: .3.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02060}02060 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_MAN is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02061}02061 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02062}02062 MAN\_EXTENSION          = .3}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02063}02063 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02064}02064 \# The MAN\_SUBDIR tag determines the name of the directory created within}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02065}02065 \# MAN\_OUTPUT in which the man pages are placed. If defaults to man followed by}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02066}02066 \# MAN\_EXTENSION with the initial . removed.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02067}02067 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_MAN is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02068}02068 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02069}02069 MAN\_SUBDIR             =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02070}02070 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02071}02071 \# If the MAN\_LINKS tag is set to YES and doxygen generates man output, then it}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02072}02072 \# will generate one additional man file for each entity documented in the real}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02073}02073 \# man page(s). These additional files only source the real man page, but without}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02074}02074 \# them the man command would be unable to find the correct page.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02075}02075 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02076}02076 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_MAN is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02077}02077 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02078}02078 MAN\_LINKS              = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02079}02079 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02080}02080 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02085}02085 \# captures the structure of the code including all documentation.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02090}02090 \# The XML\_OUTPUT tag is used to specify where the XML pages will be put. If a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02091}02091 \# relative path is entered the value of OUTPUT\_DIRECTORY will be put in front of}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02093}02093 \# The default directory is: xml.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02097}02097 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02098}02098 \# If the XML\_PROGRAMLISTING tag is set to YES, doxygen will dump the program}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02099}02099 \# listings (including syntax highlighting and cross-\/referencing information) to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02100}02100 \# the XML output. Note that enabling this will significantly increase the size}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02101}02101 \# of the XML output.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02102}02102 \# The default value is: YES.}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02132}02132 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02133}02133 \# Configuration options for the AutoGen Definitions output}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02134}02134 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02135}02135 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02136}02136 \# If the GENERATE\_AUTOGEN\_DEF tag is set to YES, doxygen will generate an}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02137}02137 \# AutoGen Definitions (see http://autogen.sourceforge.net/) file that captures}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02138}02138 \# the structure of the code including all documentation. Note that this feature}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02139}02139 \# is still experimental and incomplete at the moment.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02140}02140 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02141}02141 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02142}02142 GENERATE\_AUTOGEN\_DEF   = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02143}02143 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02144}02144 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02145}02145 \# Configuration options related to the Perl module output}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02146}02146 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02147}02147 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02148}02148 \# If the GENERATE\_PERLMOD tag is set to YES, doxygen will generate a Perl module}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02149}02149 \# file that captures the structure of the code including all documentation.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02150}02150 \#}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02151}02151 \# Note that this feature is still experimental and incomplete at the moment.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02152}02152 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02153}02153 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02154}02154 GENERATE\_PERLMOD       = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02155}02155 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02156}02156 \# If the PERLMOD\_LATEX tag is set to YES, doxygen will generate the necessary}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02157}02157 \# Makefile rules, Perl scripts and LaTeX code to be able to generate PDF and DVI}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02158}02158 \# output from the Perl module output.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02159}02159 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02160}02160 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_PERLMOD is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02161}02161 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02162}02162 PERLMOD\_LATEX          = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02163}02163 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02164}02164 \# If the PERLMOD\_PRETTY tag is set to YES, the Perl module output will be nicely}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02165}02165 \# formatted so it can be parsed by a human reader. This is useful if you want to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02166}02166 \# understand what is going on. On the other hand, if this tag is set to NO, the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02167}02167 \# size of the Perl module output will be much smaller and Perl will parse it}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02168}02168 \# just the same.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02169}02169 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02170}02170 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_PERLMOD is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02171}02171 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02172}02172 PERLMOD\_PRETTY         = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02173}02173 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02174}02174 \# The names of the make variables in the generated doxyrules.make file are}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02175}02175 \# prefixed with the string contained in PERLMOD\_MAKEVAR\_PREFIX. This is useful}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02176}02176 \# so different doxyrules.make files included by the same Makefile don't}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02177}02177 \# overwrite each other's variables.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02178}02178 \# This tag requires that the tag GENERATE\_PERLMOD is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02179}02179 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02180}02180 PERLMOD\_MAKEVAR\_PREFIX =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02181}02181 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02182}02182 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02183}02183 \# Configuration options related to the preprocessor}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02184}02184 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02185}02185 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02186}02186 \# If the ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING tag is set to YES, doxygen will evaluate all}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02187}02187 \# C-\/preprocessor directives found in the sources and include files.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02188}02188 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02189}02189 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02190}02190 ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING   = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02191}02191 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02192}02192 \# If the MACRO\_EXPANSION tag is set to YES, doxygen will expand all macro names}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02193}02193 \# in the source code. If set to NO, only conditional compilation will be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02194}02194 \# performed. Macro expansion can be done in a controlled way by setting}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02195}02195 \# EXPAND\_ONLY\_PREDEF to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02196}02196 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02197}02197 \# This tag requires that the tag ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02198}02198 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02199}02199 MACRO\_EXPANSION        = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02200}02200 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02201}02201 \# If the EXPAND\_ONLY\_PREDEF and MACRO\_EXPANSION tags are both set to YES then}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02202}02202 \# the macro expansion is limited to the macros specified with the PREDEFINED and}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02203}02203 \# EXPAND\_AS\_DEFINED tags.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02204}02204 \# The default value is: NO.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02205}02205 \# This tag requires that the tag ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02206}02206 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02207}02207 EXPAND\_ONLY\_PREDEF     = NO}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02208}02208 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02209}02209 \# If the SEARCH\_INCLUDES tag is set to YES, the include files in the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02210}02210 \# INCLUDE\_PATH will be searched if a \#include is found.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02211}02211 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02212}02212 \# This tag requires that the tag ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02213}02213 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02214}02214 SEARCH\_INCLUDES        = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02215}02215 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02216}02216 \# The INCLUDE\_PATH tag can be used to specify one or more directories that}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02217}02217 \# contain include files that are not input files but should be processed by the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02218}02218 \# preprocessor.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02219}02219 \# This tag requires that the tag SEARCH\_INCLUDES is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02220}02220 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02221}02221 INCLUDE\_PATH           =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02222}02222 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02223}02223 \# You can use the INCLUDE\_FILE\_PATTERNS tag to specify one or more wildcard}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02224}02224 \# patterns (like *.h and *.hpp) to filter out the header-\/files in the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02225}02225 \# directories. If left blank, the patterns specified with FILE\_PATTERNS will be}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02226}02226 \# used.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02227}02227 \# This tag requires that the tag ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02228}02228 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02229}02229 INCLUDE\_FILE\_PATTERNS  =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02230}02230 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02231}02231 \# The PREDEFINED tag can be used to specify one or more macro names that are}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02232}02232 \# defined before the preprocessor is started (similar to the -\/D option of e.g.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02233}02233 \# gcc). The argument of the tag is a list of macros of the form: name or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02234}02234 \# name=definition (no spaces). If the definition and the "{}="{} are omitted, "{}=1"{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02235}02235 \# is assumed. To prevent a macro definition from being undefined via \#undef or}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02236}02236 \# recursively expanded use the := operator instead of the = operator.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02237}02237 \# This tag requires that the tag ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02238}02238 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02239}02239 PREDEFINED             =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02240}02240 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02241}02241 \# If the MACRO\_EXPANSION and EXPAND\_ONLY\_PREDEF tags are set to YES then this}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02242}02242 \# tag can be used to specify a list of macro names that should be expanded. The}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02243}02243 \# macro definition that is found in the sources will be used. Use the PREDEFINED}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02244}02244 \# tag if you want to use a different macro definition that overrules the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02245}02245 \# definition found in the source code.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02246}02246 \# This tag requires that the tag ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02247}02247 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02248}02248 EXPAND\_AS\_DEFINED      =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02249}02249 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02250}02250 \# If the SKIP\_FUNCTION\_MACROS tag is set to YES then doxygen's preprocessor will}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02251}02251 \# remove all references to function-\/like macros that are alone on a line, have}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02252}02252 \# an all uppercase name, and do not end with a semicolon. Such function macros}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02253}02253 \# are typically used for boiler-\/plate code, and will confuse the parser if not}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02254}02254 \# removed.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02255}02255 \# The default value is: YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02256}02256 \# This tag requires that the tag ENABLE\_PREPROCESSING is set to YES.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02257}02257 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02258}02258 SKIP\_FUNCTION\_MACROS   = YES}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02259}02259 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02260}02260 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02261}02261 \# Configuration options related to external references}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02262}02262 \#-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02263}02263 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02264}02264 \# The TAGFILES tag can be used to specify one or more tag files. For each tag}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02265}02265 \# file the location of the external documentation should be added. The format of}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02266}02266 \# a tag file without this location is as follows:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02267}02267 \# TAGFILES = file1 file2 ...}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02268}02268 \# Adding location for the tag files is done as follows:}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02269}02269 \# TAGFILES = file1=loc1 "{}file2 = loc2"{} ...}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02270}02270 \# where loc1 and loc2 can be relative or absolute paths or URLs. See the}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02271}02271 \# section "{}Linking to external documentation"{} for more information about the use}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02272}02272 \# of tag files.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02273}02273 \# Note: Each tag file must have a unique name (where the name does NOT include}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02274}02274 \# the path). If a tag file is not located in the directory in which doxygen is}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02275}02275 \# run, you must also specify the path to the tagfile here.}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02276}02276 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02277}02277 TAGFILES               =}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02278}02278 }
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02279}02279 \# When a file name is specified after GENERATE\_TAGFILE, doxygen will create a}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02280}02280 \# tag file that is based on the input files it reads. See section "{}Linking to}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02281}02281 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# external documentation"{} for more information about the usage of tag files.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02282}02282 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02283}02283 \textcolor{preprocessor}{GENERATE\_TAGFILE       =}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02284}02284 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02285}02285 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# If the ALLEXTERNALS tag is set to YES, all external class will be listed in}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02286}02286 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# the class index. If set to NO, only the inherited external classes will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02287}02287 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# listed.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02288}02288 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The default value is: NO.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02289}02289 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02290}02290 \textcolor{preprocessor}{ALLEXTERNALS           = NO}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02291}02291 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02292}02292 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# If the EXTERNAL\_GROUPS tag is set to YES, all external groups will be listed}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02293}02293 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# in the modules index. If set to NO, only the current project's groups will be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02294}02294 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# listed.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02406}02406 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02407}02407 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# If the UML\_LOOK tag is enabled, the fields and methods are shown inside the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02408}02408 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# class node. If there are many fields or methods and many nodes the graph may}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02409}02409 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# become too big to be useful. The UML\_LIMIT\_NUM\_FIELDS threshold limits the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02410}02410 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# number of items for each type to make the size more manageable. Set this to 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02411}02411 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# for no limit. Note that the threshold may be exceeded by 50\% before the limit}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02412}02412 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# is enforced. So when you set the threshold to 10, up to 15 fields may appear,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02413}02413 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# but if the number exceeds 15, the total amount of fields shown is limited to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02414}02414 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# 10.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02415}02415 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# Minimum value: 0, maximum value: 100, default value: 10.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02416}02416 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# This tag requires that the tag UML\_LOOK is set to YES.}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02578}02578 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The DOT\_GRAPH\_MAX\_NODES tag can be used to set the maximum number of nodes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02579}02579 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# that will be shown in the graph. If the number of nodes in a graph becomes}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02580}02580 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# larger than this value, doxygen will truncate the graph, which is visualized}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02581}02581 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# by representing a node as a red box. Note that doxygen if the number of direct}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02582}02582 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# children of the root node in a graph is already larger than}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02583}02583 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# DOT\_GRAPH\_MAX\_NODES then the graph will not be shown at all. Also note that}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02584}02584 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# the size of a graph can be further restricted by MAX\_DOT\_GRAPH\_DEPTH.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02585}02585 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# Minimum value: 0, maximum value: 10000, default value: 50.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02586}02586 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# This tag requires that the tag HAVE\_DOT is set to YES.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02587}02587 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02588}02588 \textcolor{preprocessor}{DOT\_GRAPH\_MAX\_NODES    = 50}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02589}02589 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02590}02590 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# The MAX\_DOT\_GRAPH\_DEPTH tag can be used to set the maximum depth of the graphs}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02591}02591 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# generated by dot. A depth value of 3 means that only nodes reachable from the}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02592}02592 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# root by following a path via at most 3 edges will be shown. Nodes that lay}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02593}02593 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# further from the root node will be omitted. Note that setting this option to 1}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02594}02594 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# or 2 may greatly reduce the computation time needed for large code bases. Also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02595}02595 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# note that the size of a graph can be further restricted by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02596}02596 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# DOT\_GRAPH\_MAX\_NODES. Using a depth of 0 means no depth restriction.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02597}02597 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# Minimum value: 0, maximum value: 1000, default value: 0.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02598}02598 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# This tag requires that the tag HAVE\_DOT is set to YES.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02599}02599 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02600}02600 \textcolor{preprocessor}{MAX\_DOT\_GRAPH\_DEPTH    = 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02601}02601 \textcolor{preprocessor}{}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02603}02603 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# background. This is disabled by default, because dot on Windows does not seem}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02604}02604 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# to support this out of the box.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02605}02605 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02606}02606 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# Warning: Depending on the platform used, enabling this option may lead to}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{_p_i_d_controller_8cpp_source_l02607}02607 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\# badly anti-\/aliased labels on the edges of a graph (i.e. they become hard to}}
